   3: const TOKEN_RE = /^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]$/;
   4: 
   5: export interface ParsedToken {
   6:   raw: string;
   7:   source_id: string;
   8:   start: number;
   9:   end: number;
  10: }
  11: 
  12: export function parseProvenanceToken(token: string): ParsedToken | null {
  13:   const match = TOKEN_RE.exec(token.trim());
  14:   if (!match) return null;
  15:   return {
  16:     raw: token,
  17:     source_id: match[1],
  18:     start: parseInt(match[2], 10),
  19:     end: parseInt(match[3], 10),
  20:   };
  21: }
  22: 
  23: export function parseAllTokens(tokens: string[]): ParsedToken[] {
  24:   return tokens
  25:     .map(parseProvenanceToken)
  26:     .filter((t): t is ParsedToken => t !== null);
  27: }

  35:   question: string;
  36:   document_ids?: string[];
  37: }
  38: 
  39: export interface RunStatusResponse {
  40:   run_id: string;
  41:   status: RunStatus;
  42:   template: string;
  43:   question: string;
  44:   queued_at: string;
  45:   started_at?: string | null;
  46:   finished_at?: string | null;
  47: }
  48: 
  49: export interface ApiError extends Error {
  50:   status: number;
  51:   body: unknown;
  52: }
  53: 
  54: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
  55:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
  56:   if (!response.ok) {
  57:     const error = new Error(
  58:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
  59:     ) as ApiError;
  60:     error.status = response.status;
  61:     error.body = body;
  62:     throw error;
  63:   }
  64:   return body as T;
  65: }
  66: 
  67: export async function createRun(
  68:   payload: RunRequest,
  69: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
  70:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs`, {
  71:     method: "POST",
  72:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
  73:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  74:   });
  75:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
  76: }
  77: 
  78: export async function getRun(runId: string): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
  79:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${runId}`);
  80:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
  81: }

 109: export async function uploadDocument(
 110:   file: File,
 111:   classification: DataClassification = "UNKNOWN",
 112: ): Promise<UploadResponse> {
 113:   const form = new FormData();
 114:   form.append("file", file);
 115:   form.append("classification", classification);
 116:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/upload`, {
 117:     method: "POST",
 118:     body: form,
 119:   });
 120:   return asJsonOrThrow<UploadResponse>(response);

 557: /** Convenience: count sources matching a given tier. */
 558: export function countSourcesByTier(
 559:   pool: EvidencePool,
 560:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 561: ): number {
 562:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 563: }
 564: 
 565: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 566: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 567:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 568: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 569:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 570:     T1: 0,
 571:     T2: 1,
 572:     T3: 2,
 573:   };
 574:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 575:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 576:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 577:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 578:   });
 579: }

 297: function SectionCard({
 298:   section,
 299:   show_dropped,
 300:   hovered_id,
 301:   onSelect,
 302:   onSelectContradiction,
 303:   onSelectEvaluator,
 304:   onSelectMultiSource,
 305:   pool,
 306: }: {
 307:   section: VerifiedReportSection;
 308:   show_dropped: boolean;
 309:   hovered_id: string | null;
 310:   onSelect: (id: string, sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence) => void;
 311:   onSelectContradiction: (signal: ContradictionSignal) => void;
 312:   onSelectEvaluator: (d: EvaluatorDisagreement) => void;
 313:   onSelectMultiSource: (payload: {
 314:     tokens: ParsedToken[];
 315:     sentence_text: string;
 316:   }) => void;
 317:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
 318: }) {

 324:       className={cn(
 325:         "border",
 326:         section.section_status === "dropped" && "opacity-60",
 327:       )}
 328:     >
 329:       <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between gap-3">
 330:         <CardTitle className="text-base">{section.section_title}</CardTitle>
 331:         <span
 332:           className={cn(
 333:             "rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] tracking-widest uppercase",
 334:             STATUS_TONE[section.section_status],
 335:           )}
 336:         >
 337:           {section.section_status} ·{" "}
 338:           {Math.round(section.section_verify_pass_rate * 100)}%
 339:         </span>
 340:       </CardHeader>
 341:       <CardContent className="flex flex-col gap-2">
 342:         {kept.length === 0 && !show_dropped ? (
 343:           <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">
 344:             No verified sentences in this section.
 345:           </p>
 346:         ) : (
 347:           <ul className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
 348:             {section.verified_sentences.map((s, idx) => (
 349:               <SentenceRow
 350:                 key={idx}
 351:                 sentence={s}
 352:                 show_dropped={show_dropped}
 353:                 sentence_id={`${section.section_id}:${idx}`}
 354:                 hovered_id={hovered_id}
 355:                 onSelect={onSelect}
 356:                 onSelectContradiction={onSelectContradiction}
 357:                 onSelectEvaluator={onSelectEvaluator}
 358:                 onSelectMultiSource={onSelectMultiSource}
 359:                 pool={pool}
 360:               />
 361:             ))}
 362:           </ul>
 363:         )}
 364:         {!show_dropped && dropped_count > 0 ? (
 365:           <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs italic">
 366:             {dropped_count} sentence{dropped_count > 1 ? "s" : ""} dropped by
 367:             strict-verify (toggle below to inspect).
 368:           </p>
 369:         ) : null}
 370:       </CardContent>
 371:     </Card>
 372:   );
 373: }
 374: 
 375: export function VerifiedReportView({
 376:   report,
 377:   show_dropped = false,
 378:   pool = null,
 379: }: {
 380:   report: VerifiedReport;
 381:   show_dropped?: boolean;
 382:   pool?: EvidencePool | null;
 383: }) {
 384:   const { hovered_id, root_ref } = useSentenceHover();
 385:   const [inspector, setInspector] = useState<{
 386:     id: string;
 387:     sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence;
 388:   } | null>(null);
 389:   const [contradiction_open, set_contradiction_open] =
 390:     useState<ContradictionSignal | null>(null);
 391:   const [evaluator_open, set_evaluator_open] =
 392:     useState<EvaluatorDisagreement | null>(null);
 393:   const [multi_source_open, set_multi_source_open] = useState<{
 394:     tokens: ParsedToken[];
 395:     sentence_text: string;
 396:   } | null>(null);
 397:   return (
 398:     <div
 399:       ref={root_ref}
 400:       data-testid="verified-report-view"
 401:       className="flex flex-col gap-4"
 402:     >
 403:       <FrameCoveragePanel coverage={report.frame_coverage ?? null} />
 404:       <Card>
 405:         <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between gap-3">
 406:           <CardTitle className="text-lg">Verified report</CardTitle>
 407:           <VerdictBadge verdict={report.pipeline_verdict} />
 408:         </CardHeader>
 409:         <CardContent>
 410:           <dl className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-6 gap-y-1 text-sm">
 411:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Generator</dt>
 412:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 413:               {report.generator_model}
 414:             </dd>
 415:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Evaluator</dt>
 416:             <dd
 417:               className="text-foreground flex items-center gap-2 font-medium"
 418:               data-testid="report-evaluator"
 419:             >
 420:               {report.evaluator_model}
 421:               {report.family_segregation_passed ? (
 422:                 <span
 423:                   data-testid="family-segregated"
 424:                   title="Two-family segregation passed: evaluator and generator are from different training lineages."
 425:                   className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-emerald-700 uppercase dark:text-emerald-300"
 426:                 >
 427:                   ✓ Family segregated
 428:                 </span>
 429:               ) : (
 430:                 <span
 431:                   data-testid="family-not-segregated"
 432:                   title="Two-family segregation FAILED: evaluator and generator share training lineage."
 433:                   className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 434:                 >
 435:                   ✗ Same family
 436:                 </span>
 437:               )}
 438:             </dd>
 439:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Pass rate</dt>
 440:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 441:               {Math.round(report.overall_verify_pass_rate * 100)}%
 442:             </dd>
 443:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Sections</dt>
 444:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 445:               {
 446:                 report.sections.filter((s) => s.section_status !== "dropped")
 447:                   .length
 448:               }{" "}
 449:               kept ·{" "}
 450:               {
 451:                 report.sections.filter((s) => s.section_status === "dropped")
 452:                   .length
 453:               }{" "}
 454:               dropped
 455:             </dd>
 456:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Latency</dt>
 457:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 458:               {report.latency_ms} ms
 459:             </dd>
 460:           </dl>
 461:           <p
 462:             data-testid="assertion-surface-legend"
 463:             className="text-muted-foreground mt-3 text-xs"
 464:           >
 465:             Gated assertion surfaces (all clickable through Inspector):{" "}
 466:             {ASSERTION_SURFACES.map((s) => SURFACE_LABEL[s]).join(", ")}.
 467:           </p>
 468:         </CardContent>
 469:       </Card>
 470: 
 471:       {report.sections.map((section) => (
 472:         <SectionCard
 473:           key={section.section_id}
 474:           section={section}
 475:           show_dropped={show_dropped}
 476:           hovered_id={hovered_id}
 477:           onSelect={(id, sentence) => setInspector({ id, sentence })}
 478:           onSelectContradiction={(signal) => set_contradiction_open(signal)}
 479:           onSelectEvaluator={(d) => set_evaluator_open(d)}
 480:           onSelectMultiSource={(payload) => set_multi_source_open(payload)}
 481:           pool={pool}
 482:         />
 483:       ))}
 484:       <ContradictionPane
 485:         open={contradiction_open !== null}
 486:         signal={contradiction_open}
 487:         onOpenChange={(open) => {
 488:           if (!open) set_contradiction_open(null);
 489:         }}
 490:       />
 491:       <EvaluatorPane
 492:         open={evaluator_open !== null}
 493:         disagreement={evaluator_open}
 494:         onOpenChange={(open) => {
 495:           if (!open) set_evaluator_open(null);
 496:         }}
 497:       />
 498:       <MultiSourcePanel
 499:         open={multi_source_open !== null}
 500:         tokens={multi_source_open?.tokens ?? []}
 501:         sentence_text={multi_source_open?.sentence_text ?? ""}
 502:         pool={pool}
 503:         onOpenChange={(open) => {
 504:           if (!open) set_multi_source_open(null);
 505:         }}
 506:       />
 507:       <SentenceInspector
 508:         open={inspector !== null}
 509:         onOpenChange={(open) => {
 510:           if (!open) setInspector(null);
 511:         }}
 512:         sentence={inspector?.sentence ?? null}
 513:         sentence_id={inspector?.id ?? null}
 514:         pool={pool}
 515:       />
 516:     </div>
 517:   );
 518: }

    I-f14-005: Cited recall — 'from prior run' badge for ev_memory_* citations
    
    When a verified sentence's provenance tokens reference an evidence_id
    starting with ev_memory_ (per I-f14-004), render an inline purple chip
    below the provenance line with title='Cites prior workspace run via <ids>'.
    New /sentence_hover_test/memory_cite fixture page renders 1 memory-cite +
    1 non-memory sentence; Playwright spec asserts the badge appears for the
    former and not the latter, and title contains the ev_memory_ id.
    
    Codex APPROVE iter 1 on brief.
    
    Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
